================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

	if enabled then

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Charger/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Charger → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

		end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_18_Charger/VPD_18_Unmarked_Charger/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD 18' Charger → VPD '18 Unmarked Charger → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);

	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(1)
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	if enabled then
		local rotLights = ELSModel.RotLights;
		for i, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = true;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		end;
		while true do
			for i = 1, 360, 15 do
				for i2, v in next, rotLights:GetChildren() do
					local orientation = Vector3.new(0, v.OppositeDirection.Value and -i or i, 0);
					v.Chrome.Orientation = orientation;
					v.Light.Orientation = orientation;
				end;
				wait();
			end;
			wait();
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, ELSModel.RotLights:GetChildren() do
			v.Light.SpotLight.Enabled = false;
			v.Light.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.BrakeLights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v.Name ~= 'Top' then
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Caprice/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Caprice → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

					L7(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255));

					end
				end)
		end)
		if enabled then

				pcall(function()
					while true do
						M1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

						M4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
						M5(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
						M6(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
						M7(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
						M8(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
						wait(0.03)
						M1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;

			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;

		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Crown Victoria → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;


return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;
	
	local indicatorValue = script.Parent.Parent.State.Indicators.Value
	local indicatorOn;
	
	if indicatorValue == -1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Left;
	elseif indicatorValue == 1 then
		indicatorOn = brakelights.Right
	end

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then --If disabled and no headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	elseif headlightsState then --If disabled and headlights
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			if v ~= indicatorOn then
				v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Rearlights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();
	local indicatorRear = body.Rearlights[(side == -1) and 'Left' or 'Right'];

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = neonMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 0, 0)
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			indicatorRear.Material = smoothMaterial;
			indicatorRear.Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 65, 65);
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
		indicatorRear.Material = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Material;
		indicatorRear.Color = indicatorRear.Parent.Centre.Color;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Crown_Victoria/VPD_Unmarked_Crown_Victoria/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Crown Victoria → VPD Unmarked Crown Victoria → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_DriveSafeTeam/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD DriveSafeTeam → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local L1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L1);
	local L2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L2);
	local L3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L3);
	local L4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L4);
	local L5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L5);
	local L6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L6);
	local L7 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.L7);
	local F1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F4);
	local F5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.F7);
	local M1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M1);
	local M2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M7);
	local M8 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.M8);
	local H1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H1);
	local H2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H2);
	local H3 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H3);
	local H4 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.H4);
	local G1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.G1);
	local G2 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.G2);
	local LS1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.LS1);
	local RS1 = require(elsModule)(ELSModel.RS1);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));	
					L1(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L2(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L3(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L4(0, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L5(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L6(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					L7(1, Color3.fromRGB(110, 153, 202));
					wait(0.13)
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F5(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F6(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do

			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Marked_Explorer/Config/Modules/TdPart.lua ---

--[[
    TdPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Marked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		part.Transparency = (transparency)
		if colour then
			if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
				part.BrickColor = colour;
			elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
				part.Color = colour;
			end;
		end;
		if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
			local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
			a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
			if colour then
				a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
			end
		end;
	end;
end

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local M2 = tdModule(ELSModel.M2);
	local M3 = tdModule(ELSModel.M3);
	local M4 = tdModule(ELSModel.M4);
	local M5 = tdModule(ELSModel.M5);
	local M6 = tdModule(ELSModel.M6);
	local M7 = tdModule(ELSModel.M7);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			M7(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M6(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M5(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M4(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M3(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			M2(1);
			wait(0.3);
			M2(0, Color3.new(0.827450, 0.443137, 0.239215));
			wait(0.2);
			M7(1);
			M6(1);
			M5(1);
			M4(1);
			M3(1);
			M2(1);
		end
	else
		ELSModel.M2:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M3:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M4:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M5:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M6:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		ELSModel.M7:SetAttribute('TD', nil);
		M7(1);
		M6(1);
		M5(1);
		M4(1);
		M3(1);
		M2(1);
	end
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:51
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, headlights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
			v.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		end;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_Explorer/VPD_Unmarked_Explorer/Config/TDPatterns/Left.lua ---

--[[
    Left (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD Explorer → VPD Unmarked Explorer → Config → TDPatterns
    Parent: TDPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local tdModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.TdPart);

return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local R7 = tdModule(ELSModel.R7);
	local R6 = tdModule(ELSModel.R6);
	local R5 = tdModule(ELSModel.R5);
	local R4 = tdModule(ELSModel.R4);
	local R3 = tdModule(ELSModel.R3);
	local R2 = tdModule(ELSModel.R2);
	
	if enabled then
		ELSModel.R2:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R3:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R4:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R5:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R6:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		ELSModel.R7:SetAttribute('TD', true);
		while true do
			R7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 151, 32));
			R6(1);
			R5(1);
			R4(1);
			R3(1);
			R2(1);
			wait(0.3);

					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Vancouver_Police_Department/VPD_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]

local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Vancouver Police Department → VPD F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:52
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;
